[Failure 29] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Find the first name and gpa of the students whose gpa is lower than the average gpa of all students.
Gold DB: college_1 | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: college_3 | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT s.Fname, SUM(gc.gradepoint * c.Credits) / SUM(c.Credits) AS gpa
FROM Student s
JOIN Enrolled_in ei ON s.StuID = ei.StuID
JOIN Course c ON ei.CID = c.CID
JOIN Gradeconversion gc ON ei.Grade = gc.lettergrade
GROUP BY s.StuID, s.Fname
HAVING gpa < (SELECT SUM(gc2.gradepoint * c2.Credits) / SUM(c2.Credits)
              FROM Enrolled_in ei2
              JOIN Course c2 ON ei2.CID = c2.CID
              JOIN Gradeconversion gc2 ON ei2.Grade = gc2.lettergrade);

[Failure 134] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: What is maximum, minimum and average amount of outstanding of customer?
Gold DB: driving_school | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: customers_and_invoices | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT MAX(ft.transaction_amount) AS max_outstanding, MIN(ft.transaction_amount) AS min_outstanding, AVG(ft.transaction_amount) AS avg_outstanding FROM Financial_Transactions ft WHERE ft.transaction_type = 'Outstanding';
------------------------------------------------------------

[Failure 135] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: What is the maximum, minimum, and average amount of money outsanding for all customers?
Gold DB: driving_school | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: customers_and_orders | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    MAX(total_outstanding) AS max_outstanding,
    MIN(total_outstanding) AS min_outstanding, 
    AVG(total_outstanding) AS avg_outstanding
FROM (
    SELECT 
        c.customer_id,
        SUM(p.product_price * oi.order_quantity) AS total_outstanding
    FROM Customers c
    JOIN Customer_Orders co ON c.customer_id = co.customer_id
    JOIN Order_Items oi ON co.order_id = oi.order_id
    JOIN Products p ON oi.product_id = p.product_id
    WHERE co.order_status_code != 'completed'
    GROUP BY c.customer_id
) customer_totals;

[Failure 242] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: For each director who directed more than one movie, what are the titles and dates of release for all those movies?
Gold DB: movie_1 | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: imdb | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT m.title, m.release_year
FROM movie m
JOIN copyright c ON m.mid = c.msid
JOIN directed_by db ON c.id = db.msid
WHERE db.did IN (
    SELECT db2.did
    FROM directed_by db2
    JOIN copyright c2 ON db2.msid = c2.msid
    JOIN movie m2 ON c2.msid = m2.mid
    GROUP BY db2.did
    HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT m2.mid) > 1
)
ORDER BY db.did, m.release_year;
------------------------------------------------------------

[Failure 282] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop

Selected DB: activity_1 | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT AVG(practice_count) AS average_hours, MAX(practice_count) AS maximum_hours
FROM (
    SELECT s.StuID, COUNT(*) AS practice_count
    FROM Student s
    JOIN Participates_in pi ON s.StuID = pi.stuid
    JOIN Activity a ON pi.actid = a.actid
    WHERE a.activity_name LIKE '%team%' AND a.activity_name LIKE '%practice%'
    GROUP BY s.StuID
) AS student_practices;

Selected DB: geo | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE

Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (s1.population * 100.0 / (SELECT SUM(population) FROM state WHERE country_name = s1.country_name)) - 
    (s2.population * 100.0 / (SELECT SUM(population) FROM state WHERE country_name = s2.country_name)) 
FROM state s1, state s2 
WHERE s1.state_name LIKE 'New Jersey' AND s2.state_name LIKE 'Vermont';

Query: Among the players born before the year 1986, how many of them would remain in his position and defense while the team attacked?
Gold DB: european_football_2 | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Selected DB: match_season | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Gold SQL: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT p.id)
FROM Player p
JOIN Player_Attributes pa ON p.player_api_id = pa.player_api_id
WHERE p.birthday < '1986-01-01'
  AND pa.defensive_work_rate LIKE '%Stay Back%'
  AND pa.attacking_work_rate LIKE '%Stay Back%';
Selected SQL: SELECT COUNT(*) 
FROM match_season ms
JOIN player p ON ms.Player = p.Player
WHERE ms.Position = 'Defense' 
AND ms.Player IN (
    SELECT Player 
    FROM match_season 
    GROUP BY Player 
    HAVING MIN(Season) < 1986
);

[Failure 487] - CATEGORY: Unresolvable Ambiguity
Query: Who are the account holder identification numbers whose who have transactions on the credit card with the amount is less than the average, in 1998?
Gold DB: financial | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Selected DB: customers_card_transactions | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Gold SQL: SELECT DISTINCT d.client_id
FROM trans t
JOIN disp d ON t.account_id = d.account_id
JOIN card c ON d.disp_id = c.disp_id
WHERE t.date LIKE '1998%'
AND t.type = 'credit card'
AND t.amount < (SELECT AVG(amount) FROM trans WHERE date LIKE '1998%' AND type = 'credit card');
Selected SQL: SELECT DISTINCT c.customer_id
FROM Customers c
JOIN Accounts a ON c.customer_id = a.customer_id
JOIN Financial_Transactions ft ON a.account_id = ft.account_id
JOIN Customers_Cards cc ON ft.card_id = cc.card_id
WHERE ft.transaction_amount < (
    SELECT AVG(transaction_amount)
    FROM Financial_Transactions
    WHERE strftime('%Y', transaction_date) = '1998'
)
AND strftime('%Y', ft.transaction_date) = '1998'
AND cc.card_type_code = 'Credit';

[Failure 490] - CATEGORY: Unresolvable Ambiguity
Query: Which services type had both successful and failure event details?
Gold DB: local_govt_in_alabama | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Selected DB: e_government | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Gold SQL: SELECT DISTINCT s.Service_Type_Code
FROM Services s
JOIN Events e ON s.Service_ID = e.Service_ID
WHERE e.Event_Details LIKE '%successful%' 
AND s.Service_ID IN (
    SELECT s2.Service_ID
    FROM Services s2
    JOIN Events e2 ON s2.Service_ID = e2.Service_ID
    WHERE e2.Event_Details LIKE '%failure%'
);
Selected SQL: SELECT DISTINCT s.service_type_code
FROM Services s
JOIN Party_Services ps ON s.service_id = ps.service_id
JOIN Party_Forms pf ON ps.customer_id = pf.party_id
WHERE pf.form_status_code IN ('successful', 'failure')
GROUP BY s.service_type_code
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT pf.form_status_code) = 2;

Gold DB: scholar | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Selected DB: academic | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Gold SQL: SELECT p.paperId, p.title, COUNT(cite.citedPaperId) AS citation_count
FROM paper p
JOIN cite ON p.paperId = cite.citedPaperId
JOIN paperKeyphrase pk ON p.paperId = pk.paperId
JOIN keyphrase k ON pk.keyphraseId = k.keyphraseId
WHERE k.keyphraseName LIKE '%Artificial Intelligence%'
GROUP BY p.paperId, p.title

LIMIT 10;

WHERE d.name LIKE '%Artificial Intelligence%'

Selected DB: icfp_1 | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Gold SQL: SELECT DISTINCT a2.authorName
FROM author a1
JOIN writes w1 ON a1.authorId = w1.authorId
JOIN writes w2 ON w1.paperId = w2.paperId
JOIN author a2 ON w2.authorId = a2.authorId
WHERE a1.authorName LIKE '%Ameet Soni%' AND a2.authorName NOT LIKE '%Ameet Soni%'
INTERSECT

FROM author a1
JOIN writes w1 ON a1.authorId = w1.authorId
JOIN writes w2 ON w1.paperId = w2.paperId

JOIN Authorship au2 ON au1.paperID = au2.paperID
JOIN Authors a2 ON au2.authID = a2.authID
JOIN Authorship au3 ON au2.paperID = au3.paperID
JOIN Authors a3 ON au3.authID = a3.authID
WHERE (a1.fname LIKE 'Ameet' AND a1.lname LIKE 'Soni')
  AND (a2.fname LIKE 'Ras' AND a2.lname LIKE 'Bodik')

[Failure 677] - CATEGORY: Populated Trap / Other

Selected DB: college_2 | Status: VALID_STRUCTURE
Gold SQL: SELECT AVG(s.STU_GPA) FROM STUDENT s JOIN ENROLL e ON s.STU_NUM = e.STU_NUM JOIN CLASS c ON e.CLASS_CODE = c.CLASS_CODE WHERE c.CRS_CODE LIKE 'ACCT-211';
Selected SQL: SELECT AVG(CASE grade 
            WHEN 'A' THEN 4.0 
            WHEN 'A-' THEN 3.7 
            WHEN 'B+' THEN 3.3 
            WHEN 'B' THEN 3.0 
            WHEN 'B-' THEN 2.7 
            WHEN 'C+' THEN 2.3 
            WHEN 'C' THEN 2.0 
            WHEN 'C-' THEN 1.7 
            WHEN 'D+' THEN 1.3 
            WHEN 'D' THEN 1.0 
            WHEN 'D-' THEN 0.7 
            ELSE 0.0 
        END) 
FROM takes 
WHERE course_id = 'ACCT-211' AND grade IS NOT NULL;

[Failure 757] - CATEGORY: Populated Trap / Other
Query: What is the customer id, first and last name with least number of accounts.
Gold DB: customers_card_transactions | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: customers_and_invoices | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT c.customer_id, c.customer_first_name, c.customer_last_name
FROM Customers c
JOIN Accounts a ON c.customer_id = a.customer_id
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.customer_first_name, c.customer_last_name
HAVING COUNT(a.account_id) = (
    SELECT MIN(account_count)
    FROM (
        SELECT COUNT(account_id) AS account_count
        FROM Accounts
        GROUP BY customer_id
    )
)
ORDER BY c.customer_id
LIMIT 1;
Selected SQL: SELECT c.customer_id, c.customer_first_name, c.customer_last_name
FROM Customers c
JOIN Accounts a ON c.customer_id = a.customer_id
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.customer_first_name, c.customer_last_name
ORDER BY COUNT(*) ASC
LIMIT 1;

[Failure 769] - CATEGORY: Populated Trap / Other
Query: What are the ids of all products that were either ordered more than 3 times or have a cumulative amount purchased of above 80000?
Gold DB: department_store | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: customers_and_orders | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT p.product_id
FROM Products p
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT product_id, COUNT(*) AS order_count
    FROM Order_Items
    GROUP BY product_id
) o ON p.product_id = o.product_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT product_id, SUM(total_amount_purchased) AS total_purchased
    FROM Product_Suppliers
    GROUP BY product_id
) ps ON p.product_id = ps.product_id
WHERE (COALESCE(o.order_count, 0) > 3) OR (COALESCE(ps.total_purchased, 0) > 80000);
Selected SQL: SELECT product_id
FROM (
    SELECT 
        oi.product_id,
        COUNT(oi.order_item_id) AS order_count,
        SUM(oi.order_quantity * p.product_price) AS cumulative_amount
    FROM Order_Items oi
    JOIN Products p ON oi.product_id = p.product_id
    GROUP BY oi.product_id
) product_stats
WHERE order_count > 3 OR cumulative_amount > 80000;
------------------------------------------------------------

[Failure 798] - CATEGORY: Populated Trap / Other

FROM Player p

JOIN Match m ON p.player_api_id IN (
    m.home_player_1, m.home_player_2, m.home_player_3, m.home_player_4, m.home_player_5,
    m.home_player_6, m.home_player_7, m.home_player_8, m.home_player_9, m.home_player_10, m.home_player_11,
    m.away_player_1, m.away_player_2, m.away_player_3, m.away_player_4, m.away_player_5,
    m.away_player_6, m.away_player_7, m.away_player_8, m.away_player_9, m.away_player_10, m.away_player_11
)

);
